# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
To find n, take the cross product of any 2 vectors ON THE PLANE. Because they are both on the same 'x-y' plane, 
the cross product will give the vector that is normal to those two vectors, and therefore give the normal to the plane. ^XSJ0FMvi

You could technically find any vector, like AC and BC because they would still be vectors on the same plane. ^B5YqjoHq

z int ^D005DDiO

y int ^hgYVeiDy

x int ^ibYdexBz

Now we have part of our plane
 ^Mkta5mw7

Clearly the parts with coefficients lambda, and mew, are 
the direction that the vector is travelling ^X1zfcNdc
